<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+code-samples+python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+code-samples+python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.agents.complete(messages=[
        {
            "content": "Who is the best French painter? Answer in one short sentence.",
            "role": "user",
        },
    ], agent_id="<id>", stream=False)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+code-samples+curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+code-samples+curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents/completions \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "agent_id": "ipsum eiusmod",
  "messages": [
    {
      "content": "consequat do"
    }
  ]
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="frequency_penalty"
  headingId="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+frequency_penalty"
  typeInfo={{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"Min: -2","variant":"warning"},{"title":"Max: 2","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### frequency_penalty \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+frequency_penalty\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

frequency_penalty penalizes the repetition of words based on their frequency in the generated text. A higher frequency penalty discourages the model from repeating words that have already appeared frequently in the output, promoting diversity and reducing repetition.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

<DebugPlaceholder>

No examples provided

_OpenAPI example:_

```
examples:
  - MyExampleValue
```

</DebugPlaceholder>

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

<ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

_Default Value:_ `0`

</ExpandablePropertyDefaultValue>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### max_tokens \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+max_tokens\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion. The token count of your prompt plus `max_tokens` cannot exceed the model's context length.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### prefix \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+messages+assistantmessage+prefix\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Set this to `true` when adding an assistant message as prefix to condition the model response. The role of the prefix message is to force the model to start its answer by the content of the message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="presence_penalty"
  headingId="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+presence_penalty"
  typeInfo={{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"Min: -2","variant":"warning"},{"title":"Max: 2","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### presence_penalty \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+presence_penalty\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

presence_penalty determines how much the model penalizes the repetition of words or phrases. A higher presence penalty encourages the model to use a wider variety of words and phrases, making the output more diverse and creative.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

<DebugPlaceholder>

No examples provided

_OpenAPI example:_

```
examples:
  - MyExampleValue
```

  headingId="operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+stream"
  typeInfo={{"label":"boolean","linkedLabel":"boolean","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### stream \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+request+stream\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Whether to stream back partial progress. If set, tokens will be sent as data-only server-side events as they become available, with the stream terminated by a data: [DONE] message. Otherwise, the server will hold the request open until the timeout or until completion, with the response containing the full result as JSON.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### prefix \{#operation-agents_completion_v1_agents_completions_post+responses+200+application-json+choices+chatcompletionchoice+message+assistantmessage+prefix\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Set this to `true` when adding an assistant message as prefix to condition the model response. The role of the prefix message is to force the model to start its answer by the content of the message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
